GT Equivalence Verification (BPG22)
============================================================
GT: c0*(c1 - exp(-c2*P))*P + c3*P*exp(-c4*t)
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed):  
\[
f(t,P)=a(1-e^{-kP})P + a\,P\,e^{-kt}
\]
with \(a=0.1178160925\), \(k=0.02722849124\).  
Key structural facts:

- **Always proportional to \(P\)**: \(f(t,0)=0\) and \(f(t,P)/P = a(1-e^{-kP}) + a e^{-kt}\).
- **\(t\)-dependence** is **exactly** \(P\cdot(\text{constant})\cdot e^{-kt}\) plus a term independent of \(t\).
- **\(P\)-dependence** includes the specific nonlinearity \(P(1-e^{-kP}) = P - P e^{-kP}\): it contains both a linear-in-\(P\) part and a \(P e^{-kP}\) part with the **same** rate \(k\) as the \(t\)-exponential.

So any matching candidate must be able (possibly after setting some parameters to 0) to produce exactly:
- a term \( \alpha P\)
- a term \(-\alpha P e^{-kP}\)
- a term \(+\alpha P e^{-kt}\)
with the same \(\alpha\) and same \(k\) in the two exponentials (one in \(P\), one in \(t\)), and no extra \(t\)-rational/log/sin/etc. dependence.

Now check candidates.

---

### 1
Has only rational-in-\(t\) factors \((c1+t)^{-1}\) and exponentials \(e^{P c3}\) multiplied by rational-in-\(t\). Cannot produce a pure \(P e^{-kt}\) term (no standalone \(e^{c t}\) multiplied by \(P\) without rational factor), and \(P\)-exponential is \(e^{+cP}\) not \(e^{-kP}\) unless set \(c3<0\), but still lacks the required additive decomposition without \((c1+t)^{-1}\). No.

### 2
Contains \(e^{c3/|P|^{1/3}}\) and a log of \(e^{P c7 + c8 t}\). Wrong functional forms (logistic/log, inverse power in exponent). No.

### 3
Mostly rational forms like \(P^6/(P^5(c1+t)) = P/(c1+t)\), plus \(P/(Pc5+1)\), plus \(e^{c7 t}/(c1+t)\), plus constant \(c9\). Cannot form \(P(1-e^{-kP})\) nor \(P e^{-kt}\) cleanly. No.

### 4
Has \(P^2/(P^2+c1)\), \(t/(c3+t)\), and \(\log(1+c5 e^{Pc6+c7 t})\). Not match. No.

### 5
Rational-in-\(t\) plus \(e^{P c8}\log(c9 t+1)\). GT has no logs and no rational-in-\(t\). No.

### 6

### 9

aP - aP e^{-kP} + aP e^{-kt}

which equals GT. Domain conditions: none needed (works for all real \(t,P\)).
